import os
import librosa
import soundfile as sf
from datasets import load_dataset

# Define the target number of samples
target_sample_count = 20000
output_path = "./common_voice_fr"
os.makedirs(f"{output_path}/wavs", exist_ok=True)

# Load the validated subset of Common Voice French
dataset = load_dataset("mozilla-foundation/common_voice_11_0", "fr", split="train")

entries = []
for idx, sample in enumerate(dataset):
    if idx >= target_sample_count:
        print(f"Reached target sample count: {target_sample_count}")
        break

    if sample["audio"]["array"] is not None and sample["sentence"] is not None:
        # Resample to 24kHz (required by XTTS)
        audio_data = sample["audio"]["array"]
        sr = sample["audio"]["sampling_rate"]
        resampled_audio = librosa.resample(audio_data, orig_sr=sr, target_sr=24000)

        wav_path = f"{output_path}/wavs/sample_{idx:06d}.wav"
        sf.write(wav_path, resampled_audio, 24000)

        # Save transcription
        text = sample["sentence"].strip().replace("|", " ")
        # Add language code 'fr' at the end if needed: "sample_xxxxxx.wav|text|fr"
        # If the formatter doesn't need language code inline, just text is fine
        entries.append(f"sample_{idx:06d}.wav|{text}|fr")

# Write metadata.csv
metadata_path = f"{output_path}/metadata.csv"
with open(metadata_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write("\n".join(entries))

print(f"Common Voice French dataset prepared with {len(entries)} samples at {output_path}.")

# DVAE and MEL norm links
DVAE_CHECKPOINT_LINK = "https://coqui.gateway.scarf.sh/hf-coqui/XTTS-v1/v1.1.2/dvae.pth"
MEL_NORM_LINK = "https://coqui.gateway.scarf.sh/hf-coqui/XTTS-v1/v1.1.2/mel_stats.pth"

import os

# Define the path to your metadata file
input_metadata_path = "./common_voice_fr/metadata.csv"
output_metadata_path = "./common_voice_fr/cleaned_metadata.csv"

# Read the metadata file
with open(input_metadata_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

# Process each line to remove the language code
cleaned_lines = []
for line in lines:
    # Split by "|" and take only the first two columns (audio path and transcription)
    parts = line.strip().split("|")
    if len(parts) >= 2:
        cleaned_lines.append(f"{parts[0]}|{parts[1]}")

# Write the cleaned lines back to a new metadata file
with open(output_metadata_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write("\n".join(cleaned_lines))

print(f"Cleaned metadata file saved at {output_metadata_path}")
Cleaned metadata file saved at ./common_voice_fr/cleaned_metadata.csv
import os

# Define the path to your metadata file
input_metadata_path = "./common_voice_fr/cleaned_metadata.csv"
output_metadata_path = "./common_voice_fr/normalized_metadata.csv"

# Read the metadata file
with open(input_metadata_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

# Process each line to add a third column
normalized_lines = []
for line in lines:
    # Split by "|" and duplicate the transcription as normalized transcription
    parts = line.strip().split("|")
    if len(parts) == 2:
        normalized_lines.append(f"{parts[0]}|{parts[1]}|{parts[1]}")  # Duplicate the transcription

# Write the normalized lines back to a new metadata file
with open(output_metadata_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write("\n".join(normalized_lines))

print(f"Normalized metadata file saved at {output_metadata_path}")
Normalized metadata file saved at ./common_voice_fr/normalized_metadata.csv
import torch
from TTS.config.shared_configs import BaseDatasetConfig
from TTS.tts.datasets import load_tts_samples
from TTS.tts.layers.xtts.trainer.gpt_trainer import GPTArgs, GPTTrainer, GPTTrainerConfig, XttsAudioConfig
from trainer import Trainer, TrainerArgs

# Ensure CUDA
device = torch.device("cuda" if torch.cuda.is_available() else "cpu")
print("Using device:", device)

RUN_NAME = "GPT_XTTS_French_FT"
PROJECT_NAME = "XTTS_trainer_fr"
DASHBOARD_LOGGER = "tensorboard"
LOGGER_URI = None

OPTIMIZER_WD_ONLY_ON_WEIGHTS = True
START_WITH_EVAL = True
BATCH_SIZE = 3
GRAD_ACUMM_STEPS = 84

# Update dataset config for the French dataset
config_dataset = BaseDatasetConfig(
    formatter="ljspeech",  # use mozilla_common_voice if the formatter supports it, else ljspeech-like format
    dataset_name="common_voice_french",
    path="./common_voice_fr/",
    meta_file_train="./ljspeech_metadata_fixed.csv",
    language="fr",
)

DATASETS_CONFIG_LIST = [config_dataset]

# Model arguments
model_args = GPTArgs(
    max_conditioning_length=132300,  # 6 secs
    min_conditioning_length=66150,   # 3 secs
    debug_loading_failures=False,
    max_wav_length=255995,           # ~11.6 seconds
    max_text_length=200,
    mel_norm_file=MEL_NORM_FILE,
    dvae_checkpoint=DVAE_CHECKPOINT,
    xtts_checkpoint=XTTS_CHECKPOINT,
    tokenizer_file=TOKENIZER_FILE,
    gpt_num_audio_tokens=8194,
    gpt_start_audio_token=8192,
    gpt_stop_audio_token=8193,
    # specify language if needed
)

audio_config = XttsAudioConfig(sample_rate=22050, dvae_sample_rate=22050, output_sample_rate=24000)

config = GPTTrainerConfig(
    output_path=OUT_PATH,
    model_args=model_args,
    run_name=RUN_NAME,
    project_name=PROJECT_NAME,
    run_description="GPT XTTS training (French)",
    dashboard_logger=DASHBOARD_LOGGER,
    logger_uri=LOGGER_URI,
    audio=audio_config,
    batch_size=BATCH_SIZE,
    batch_group_size=48,
    eval_batch_size=BATCH_SIZE,
    num_loader_workers=8,
    eval_split_max_size=256,
    print_step=50,
    plot_step=100,
    log_model_step=1000,
    save_step=10000,
    save_n_checkpoints=1,
    save_checkpoints=True,
    optimizer="AdamW",
    optimizer_wd_only_on_weights=OPTIMIZER_WD_ONLY_ON_WEIGHTS,
    optimizer_params={"betas": [0.9, 0.96], "eps": 1e-8, "weight_decay": 1e-2},
    lr=5e-06,
    lr_scheduler="MultiStepLR",
    lr_scheduler_params={"milestones": [50000 * 18, 150000 * 18, 300000 * 18], "gamma": 0.5, "last_epoch": -1},
    test_sentences=[
{
    "text": "Bonjour tout le monde, comment allez-vous?",
    "speaker_wav": ["./common_voice_fr/wavs/sample_000001.wav"],  # Replace with a valid path
    "language": "fr",
},
        {
            "text": "Ceci est un test en français pour le modèle XTTS.",
            "speaker_wav": ["./common_voice_fr/wavs/sample_000001.wav"],
            "language": "fr",
        },
    ],

)

model = GPTTrainer.init_from_config(config).to(device)

# Load training samples
train_samples, eval_samples = load_tts_samples(
    DATASETS_CONFIG_LIST,
    eval_split=True,
    eval_split_max_size=config.eval_split_max_size,
    eval_split_size=config.eval_split_size,
)

# The Trainer class internally moves data to device, but if needed you can handle that here.
# Ensure that the trainer or model training steps run on GPU by verifying the trainer code.

trainer = Trainer(
    TrainerArgs(
        restore_path=None,
        skip_train_epoch=False,
        start_with_eval=START_WITH_EVAL,
        grad_accum_steps=GRAD_ACUMM_STEPS,
    ),
    config,
    output_path=OUT_PATH,
    model=model,
    train_samples=train_samples,
    eval_samples=eval_samples  # If Trainer supports a device argument, pass it here
)
